Klaviyo already has APIs for storing data and sending communications, primarily for e-commerce applications, but we’re just getting started! In 2022, Klaviyo did a major overhaul of its API foundation to align to industry standards for REST, rate-limiting, and authorization scopes. Desire to be judged on measurable outcomes and change process to achieve those outcomes\n• Experience talking to customers and listening deeply to their wants and needs\n\nThe pay range for this role is listed below.
